name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

posted:Posted February 4, 2024
msg:This one-week ski trip to Chongli was really fun, and it can be said that it exceeded my expectations. The overall service, facilities, and convenience of Chongli are very good!

This time I stayed in a total of 3 hotels, namely the Crown Hotel in Cuiyun Mountain, the Dragon Palace Hotel in Wanlong, and the Paston Hotel in Taiwu Town.

Crown Hotel in Cuiyun Mountain:
1. The hardware conditions are very good. When we checked in at night, because the room type we booked was fully booked, the front desk upgraded us to a family room, which was large and comfortable.
2. The ski resort in Cuiyun Mountain is actually very good. It is enough for beginners and intermediate players like us. This ski resort is our favorite among the three ski resorts we have visited.
3. The shortcoming of the Crown Hotel is that the hotel‚Äôs all-day dining restaurant is very average and does not match the Crown Hotel brand at all. There are only simple meals at noon and evening. The small hot pot set menu has very average ingredients, the seafood is not fresh, and the luncheon meat is very The low-quality kind, the mutton is also full of fat. By the way, can you guess what the garlic-like thing in the photo is? According to them, it is Saba fish! Oh my god, I don‚Äôt even dare to pinch it! The simple beef noodles are the kind that have been frozen for a long time and taste like chewing rubber. I hope Crown Hotel can improve the restaurant.
4. Although the restaurant is not good, this trip to Chongli made me feel very good, and I will still give Crown Hotel a good review.


Dragon Palace Hotel in Wanlong:
1. The Dragon Palace Hotel is an older hotel, and it is really incomparable with the new hotel rooms. I think the boss of Wanlong should also be aware of this, so he tries his best to make the facilities as perfect as possible: the shower is very It is convenient and easy to use, the toilet seat is electric, the toiletries are from L'Occitane, the heating is floor heating, the ski hall is equipped with a VIP lounge for hotel guests, etc.
2. One problem with the Dragon Palace Hotel is that the room is very hot and can reach 27 degrees indoors. We can only ask the maintenance man to reduce our floor heating to the lowest level. Even so, after we stayed for two days, my lips were completely dry. Bleeding.
3. The hotel buffet at Dragon Palace Hotel is just okay, and the price/performance ratio is acceptable.
4. The service at Wanlong Ski Resort is still very good, especially the front desk of the coaching school. They will patiently help you answer any questions you have. However, there is an inconvenience in skiing, that is, you need to open a lot of cards to ski. The three of us Personally, I need to bring 10 cards (2 hotel room cards, 2 temporary school equipment cards, 3 ski cards, 3 school equipment rental cards)!
5. I am actually a person who is picky about the hardware conditions of hotels, but in the end I am still willing to give Dragon Palace Hotel high marks because I am very happy here.


Paston Hotel in Taiwu Town:
  1. The room at the Paston Hotel is very large and has very good hardware conditions. It feels like home. We stayed for two nights and just wanted to lie in the room and watch TV. The sofa can be extended to become a sofa bed, and we can sit on it. very comfortable. 
  2. The hotel‚Äôs all-day restaurant is very good, cost-effective, and the service is very good.
3. The hotel's ski lobby will be equipped with an exclusive cabinet for each room. The cabinet is large and comfortable to use. I would like to express my special thanks to a male colleague at the front desk of the hotel. After he learned that I had problems using the cabinet, he took the initiative to accompany me to the ski hall and helped me fix everything from end to end. Thank you to him.
4. The management of Taiwu Ski Resort is not as good as that of the other two ski resorts. There are many unofficial coaches on the ski resort doing private work. This is actually very risky. First, if there is a safety issue of injury, who should you go to for compensation? Second, if some criminals pretend to be private tutors for 1v1, but are actually abducting children, it is difficult to avoid it.
5. There is an ice and snow amusement park in Taiwu Town. Even if you buy tickets to play in most of the activities, you still have to pay. I personally feel that it is not worth it.
6. We went to eat the hot dogs in Taiwu Town. They were quite good and the boss was also very nice. I feel like the service attitude at the craft brewery is cold. After entering their door three times, the waiter who comes to you will just look at you and leave without even greeting you. Maybe they have received more foreigners and are more open-minded.

In general, the whole family agreed that this trip to Chongli was very happy, and there were basically no regrets or troubles. I hope Chongli will get better and better!

msg:I stayed for 5 nights during the Spring Festival, and it felt very average. The price/performance ratio is extremely low. The only advantage of the basic room type this time is the sun, which is sunny during the day. The room is small, with a balcony, a bathtub, a single sink, and a small sofa. Reminder, there are only 20 rooms with sofa beds in the hotel. If you need your child to sleep on the sofa bed alone, you must tell the hotel in advance, otherwise you will not be able to change rooms midway. We stayed in the next few days and there were much fewer guests, so we didn't change them.

Breakfast and evening buffet are okay, 188 for adults and half price for children. Basically no waiting. The order is also good. There are KFC and Costa Coffee on the Crown side, both of which are open until 4/5 o'clock. The lobby bar sells bread, 20/piece, which is quite big and tastes good.

It's unbelievable that there are only three elevators in such a huge hotel. Every day I have to wait for a long time to take the elevator, and the few times I come, it is full and unable to get up. Holiday Inn Express and Crowne Plaza are in the same building. When the elevator on our floor goes to the left, Crowne Plaza is on the right, and it is connected. The ski hall is also the same. In fact, instead of living in such a cost-effective Crown, it is better to spend less money to live in Zhixuan. There is nothing different except for the room and breakfast. Both have access to Crown facilities.

This hotel is so good that I don't even want to come to Cuiyun Mountain again. Cuiyun Mountain has a total of 12 snow trails, some of which will freeze in the afternoon. I used to live in Wanlong, and I saw that the snow field has been making snow, and the snow machine is running every day. There has been no snow making here, but there is a snow machine at the foot of the mountain, and I don't know where it is making snow.

When asking for a coach, the coach counter said that the veneer only has low-level and high-level coaches. When you pay in the mini program, you find that there is no option for low-level coaches at all. The prices of low-level coaches that the counter finds for you are all the prices of intermediate-level coaches, which is a disguised price increase. I can also understand that the ski resort relies on these few months to make money. But the coaches are really uneven, basically they are college students who come to work during the holidays. Some have better qualities, positive attitudes, and can teach something. Some are just skating on the side and blocking the way. It depends on which coach you choose.

This crown is really too ordinary, not recommended.
